06605: function opsRange(arr,field,from,to){return (arr||[]).filter(x=>{const d=String(x[field]||'').slice(0,10);return(!from||d>=from)&&(!to||d<=to);});}
06606: function opsSalesDeclarationRows(from,to){const rows=new Map();opsRange(OPS.deliveries,'date',from,to).filter(x=>x.status!=='returned').forEach(d=>{const employeeId=d.employeeId||opsCli(d.clientId)?.rep||'',key=employeeId||'unassigned',r=rows.get(key)||{employeeId,employee:opsEmp(employeeId)?.name||'غير مسند',invoices:0,concrete:0,blocks:0,cash:0,transfer:0,credit:0,total:0};r.invoices++;if(/خرسان/.test(opsNormArabic(d.product)))r.concrete+=Number(d.quantity||0);if(/بل[وؤ]ك/.test(opsNormArabic(d.product)))r.blocks+=Number(d.quantity||0);r.cash+=Number(d.cash||0);r.transfer+=Number(d.transfer||0);r.credit+=Number(d.credit||0);r.total+=Number(d.amount||0);rows.set(key,r);});return [...rows.values()].sort((a,b)=>b.total-a.total);}

06711: function opsHeaderIndex(row,words){const N=row.map(opsNormArabic),W=words.map(opsNormArabic);for(const w of W){const i=N.findIndex(x=>x===w);if(i>=0)return i;}for(const w of W){const i=N.findIndex(x=>x.includes(w));if(i>=0)return i;}return -1;}
06712: function opsExcelDate(rows){const dates=[];for(const row of rows.slice(0,25))for(const cell of row){const s=String(cell||'');for(const m of s.matchAll(/(\d{1,2})[-\/]([0-1]?\d)[-\/](20\d{2})/g)){const iso=`${m[3]}-${String(m[2]).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(m[1]).padStart(2,'0')}`;if(!Number.isNaN(new Date(iso).getTime()))dates.push(iso);}}return dates.sort()[0]||'';}
